Complex CSI computation: int8 I/Q → float64 complex → amplitude/phase\n43\t  - RSSI normalization (AGC compensation): `norm = 10^((rssi_ref - rssi)/20)`\n44\t  - Spatial phase unwrapping: correct 2π jumps between adjacent subcarriers\n45\t  - Linear regression (OLS): fit `phase = a*k + b` over data subcarriers\n46\t  - STO/CFO removal: residual phase = unwrapped - (slope × k + intercept)\n47\t  - HT20 subcarrier map: 64 total, 46 data (excluding null, guard, pilot)\n48\t\n49\t- **Baseline system (`signal/baseline.go`):**\n50\t  - EMA baseline per link per subcarrier: `baseline = α×amplitude + (1-α)×baseline`\n51\t  - α = dt / (τ + dt) ≈ 0.0033 for dt=0.1s, τ=30s\n52\t  - Motion-gated updates: only update when smoothDeltaRMS < 0.05\n53\t  - Confidence scoring: 0.3 for stale baselines (>7 days), asymptotically → 1.0\n54\t  - Snapshot/restore for SQLite persistence\n55\t  - BaselineManager for multi-link coordination\n56\t\n57\t- **Motion detection (`signal/features.go`):**\n58\t  - NBVI (Normalized Bandwidth Variance Index): `Var(amp) / Mean(amp)²`\n59\t  - Welford's online algorithm for numerically stable variance\n60\t  - Top-16 subcarrier selection by NBVI score\n61\t  - deltaRMS: `sqrt(mean((amp - baseline)²))` over selected subcarriers\n62\t  - Exponential smoothing: `smooth = 0.3×raw + 0.7×prev`\n63\t  - Motion threshold: smoothDeltaRMS > 0.02\n64\t\n65\t- **Link processor (`signal/processor.go`):**\n66\t  - Complex CSI computation: int8 I/Q → float64 complex → amplitude/phase\n  - RSSI normalization (AGC compensation): `norm = 10^((rssi_ref - rssi)/20)`\n  - Spatial phase unwrapping: correct 2π jumps between adjacent subcarriers\n  - Linear regression (OLS): fit `phase = a*k + b` over data subcarriers\n  - STO/CFO removal: residual phase = unwrapped - (slope × k + intercept)\n  - HT20 subcarrier map: 64 total, 46 data (excluding null, guard, pilot)\n\n- **Baseline system (`signal/baseline.go`):**\n  - EMA baseline per link per subcarrier: `baseline = α×amplitude + (1-α)×baseline`\n  - α = dt / (τ + dt) ≈ 0.0033 for dt=0.1s, τ=30s\n  - Motion-gated updates: only update when smoothDeltaRMS < 0.05\n  - Confidence scoring: 0.3 for stale baselines (>7 days), asymptotically → 1.0\n  - Snapshot/restore for SQLite persistence\n  - BaselineManager for multi-link coordination\n\n- **Motion detection (`signal/features.go`):**\n  - NBVI (Normalized Bandwidth Variance Index): `Var(amp) / Mean(amp)²`\n  - Welford's online algorithm for numerically stable variance\n  - Top-16 subcarrier selection by NBVI score\n  - deltaRMS: `sqrt(mean((amp - baseline)²))` over selected subcarriers\n  - Exponential smoothing: `smooth = 0.3×raw + 0.7×prev`\n  - Motion threshold: smoothDeltaRMS > 0.02\n\n- **Link processor (`signal/processor.go`):**\n  - LinkProcessor: ties together phase sanitization, baseline, motion detection\n  - ProcessorManager: manages per-link processors with thread-safe access\n  - GetAllMotionStates(): returns motion state for all links\n  - GetAllBaselines()/RestoreBaseline(): for SQLite persistence\n\n**Constants used (from plan):**\n- RSSIRefdBm = -30.0\n- DefaultMotionThreshold = 0.05\n- DefaultDeltaRMSThreshold = 0.02\n- NBVITopCount = 16\n- NBVIMinThreshold = 0.001\n- DeltaRMSSmoothingAlpha = 0.3\n\n**Tests:** 37 tests covering phase sanitization, baseline, NBVI, motion detection. Validation: min/max length, payload size match, channel validity (1-14), subcarrier limit (128)\n  - Malformed frame tracking with warn/close thresholds (100/1000 per minute)\n- **JSON message handling:** Parses hello, health, ble, motion_hint, ota_status\n- **Per-link ring buffers:** 256-sample circular buffers keyed by `nodeMAC:peerMAC`\n- **Connection lifecycle:** Node registration via hello, ping/pong keepalive (30s/60s), graceful shutdown\n- **mDNS advertisement:** `_spaxel._tcp.local` via github.com/hashicorp/mdns\n- **Role/config push:** Sends initial `rx` role and 20 Hz config on connect\n- **Health endpoint:** `GET /healthz` returns `{\"status\":\"ok\",\"version\":\"...\"}`\n\n**Dependencies used:**\n- `github.com/go-chi/chi` — HTTP routing\n- `github.com/gorilla/websocket` — WebSocket server\n- `github.com/hashicorp/mdns` — mDNS advertisement\n\n**Tests:** 22 tests covering frame parsing, JSON messages, and ring buffer operations. tracking (`prediction/model.go`):**\n  - `zone_transitions_history` table with all zone transitions (person_id, from_zone, to_zone, hour_of_week, dwell_duration)\n  - `transition_probabilities` table with Laplace-smoothed probabilities\n  - `dwell_times` table with mean/stddev dwell time per person/zone/hour\n  - `person_zone_entry` table for tracking current person positions\n  - Zone transition recording via `PersonZoneChange()` method\n  - Automatic probability recomputation with Laplace smoothing\n  - Dwell time statistics with mean/stddev computation\n\n- **Per-zone occupancy patterns (`prediction/accuracy.go`):**\n  - `zone_occupancy_patterns` table with occupancy_prob per zone/hour_of_week\n  - `zone_occupancy_history` table tracking entries/exits with timestamps\n  - `recorded_predictions` table for tracking prediction accuracy\n  - `accuracy_stats` table with rolling 7-day accuracy metrics\n  - Zone occupancy pattern computation from historical data\n  - Pattern-based occupancy prediction at target time\n\n- **Time-slot based predictions (`prediction/horizon.go`):**\n  - Monte Carlo simulation with 1000 runs for probabilistic predictions\n  - Multi-step path simulation accounting for dwell times\n  - Normal distribution sampling for dwell time variability\n  - Horizon predictions at 5, 15, and 30 minutes\n  - Returns probability distribution over all zones\n  - Confidence scoring based on simulation agreement\n\n- **HA sensor exposure (`mqtt/client.go`):**\n  - `PublishPredictionSensors()` creates HA auto-discovery configs\n  - `UpdatePredictionState()` publishes current predictions to MQTT\n  - Three sensors per person:\n    - `sensor.spaxel_<person>_predicted_zone` - zone name\n    - `sensor.spaxel_<person>_prediction_confidence` - percentage\n    - `sensor.spaxel_<person>_transition_minutes` - estimated minutes\n  - Topics follow HA discovery pattern: `homeassistant/sensor/.../config`\n\n- **REST API endpoints (`api/prediction.go`):**\n  - `GET /api/predictions` - Get current predictions for all people\n  - `GET /api/predictions?person=<id>&horizon=<min>` - Filtered predictions\n  - `GET /api/predictions/stats` - Transition count, data age, model readiness\n  - `POST /api/predictions/recompute` - Force probability recomputation\n  - `GET /api/predictions/accuracy` - Per-person accuracy stats\n  - `GET /api/predictions/accuracy/overall` - Overall system accuracy\n  - `GET /api/predictions/accuracy/{personID}` - Person-specific accuracy\n  - `GET /api/predictions/horizon` - Monte Carlo horizon predictions\n  - `GET /api/predictions/horizon/{personID}` - Person-specific horizon prediction\n  - `GET /api/predictions/patterns/zones` - Zone occupancy patterns\n  - `GET /api/predictions/probabilities/{personID}` - Transition probabilities\n  - `GET /api/predictions/samples/{personID}/zone/{zoneID}` - Sample counts\n\n- **Main application wiring (`cmd/mothership/main.go`):**\n  - Prediction module initialization (lines 492-534)\n  - Zone transition recording on portal crossings (lines 1579-1581)\n  - Provider wiring for zones, people, positions (lines 1831-1863)\n  - MQTT client integration for prediction publishing (lines 1846-1863)\n  - Periodic prediction update loop every 60 seconds (lines 1866-1888)\n  - Periodic prediction evaluation every 30 seconds (lines 1931-1983)\n  - REST API endpoint registration (lines 2527-2888)\n\n**Constants and thresholds:**\n- MinimumDataAge = 7 days (168 hours) before predictions activate\n- MinimumSamplesPerSlot = 3 observations per time slot\n- PredictionHorizon = 15 minutes (default)\n- MonteCarloRuns = 1000 simulations\n- TargetAccuracy = 75% at 15-minute horizon\n\n**Accuracy tracking:**\n- Records predictions when made (personID, currentZone, predictedZone, confidence, horizon)\n- Evaluates pending predictions when target time is reached\n- Compares predicted zone vs actual zone\n- Computes rolling 7-day accuracy percentage\n- Reports \"meets_target\" when accuracy ≥ 75% and min predictions threshold met\n\n**Model learning:**\n- Observations recorded every 5 minutes per person/zone\n- EMA update: `p_new = p_old + α × (obs - p_old)` where α = 0.03\n- Cold start: 7 days of data required for model readiness\n- Slot ready when sample_count ≥ 3\n- Automatic recomputation triggered on zone transitions\n\n**Files propagation model with path loss + wall penetration + first-order reflections\n- GDOP computation per cell using Fisher information matrix\n- REST API at `/api/simulator/*` for space/node/walker management and GDOP computation\n\n**CSI simulator CLI (`cmd/sim/`):**\n- Connects to mothership as virtual nodes, sends synthetic CSI binary frames\n- Walker random-walk model with Gaussian velocity updates, wall reflection\n- Amplitude/phase generated from propagation model with Gaussian noise injection\n- Optional BLE advertisement simulation (`--ble` flag)\n- Verified authentication (exits non-zero on `{type:\"reject\"}`)\n- Integration test support: polls `GET /api/blobs` for blob count assertions\n\n**Fresnel zone debug overlay (`dashboard/js/fresnel.js`):**\n- Toggle-able wireframe ellipsoids between active TX/RX link pairs\n- Ellipsoid geometry computed from TX/RX positions and Fresnel zone number\n- Color-coded by zone number (zone 1 = bright, outer zones = dimmer)\n- Toolbar button integration with existing layers panel\n\n**Files created/modified:**\n```\nmothership/internal/timeline/       — timeline.go, timeline_test.go, handler.go, expert mode only\n\n**Morning briefing (`internal/briefing/`, `dashboard/js/briefing.js`):**\n- `Generator` assembles briefing in priority order from sleep, events, anomalies, system health\n- Priority blocks: critical alerts → sleep summary → who is home → overnight anomalies → system health → predictions → learning progress\n- Degenerate case: \"All quiet last night. connectivity → show link health → suggest repositioning → offer re-baseline\n- First-time feature tooltips shown once, dismissed on click, stored in `localStorage`\n- Post-feedback explanations in timeline after incorrect/missed detection feedback\n\n**Mobile-responsive expert mode (`dashboard/js/mobile.js` + CSS):**\n- Touch orbit (one finger), pan (two fingers), pinch-zoom (two fingers)\n- FXAA anti-aliasing replaces MSAA on mobile (better performance on low-power GPUs)\n- Hamburger menu for toolbar panels on small screens\n- Viewport meta tag with `viewport-fit=cover` for notch-aware layout\n- CSS Grid layout collapses gracefully on narrow viewports\n\n**Fleet status page (`dashboard/fleet.html`, `dashboard/js/fleet-page.js`):**\n- Full table with sortable columns: Name, MAC, blob/link positions.\n356\tfunc (h *Handler) computeExplanation(blob BlobSnapshot, links []LinkState, _ *GridSnapshot) *BlobExplanation {\n357\t\texplanation := &BlobExplanation{\n358\t\t\tBlobID:            blob.ID,\n359\t\t\tX:                 blob.X,\n360\t\t\tY:                 blob.Y,\n361\t\t\tZ:                 blob.Z,\n362\t\t\tConfidence:        blob.Confidence,\n363\t\t\tContributingLinks: []LinkContribution{},\n364\t\t\tAllLinks:          make([]LinkContribution, 0, len(links)),\n365\t\t\tFresnelZones:      []FresnelZone{},\n366\t\t}\n367\t\n368\t\t// WiFi wavelength constant (2.4 GHz -> ~0.123 m)\n369\t\tconst lambda = 0.123\n370\t\tconst halfLambda = lambda / 2\n371\t\n372\t\tvar totalContribution float64\n373\t\n374\t\t// Compute raw contribution for each link\n375\t\tfor _, link := range links {\n376\t\t\tlinkID := link.NodeMAC + \":\" + link.PeerMAC\n377\t\n378\t\t\tnodePos := [3]float64{link.NodePos[0], link.NodePos[1], link.NodePos[2]}\n379\t\t\tpeerPos := [3]float64{link.PeerPos[0], link.PeerPos[1], link.PeerPos[2]}\n380\t\n381\t\t\t// Path length excess at blob position: ΔL = |blob-TX| + |blob-RX| - |TX-RX|\n382\t\t\tpathDirect := math.Sqrt(\n383\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[0]-nodePos[0], 2) +\n384\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[1]-nodePos[1], 2) +\n385\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[2]-nodePos[2], 2))\n386\t\t\tpathViaBlob := math.Sqrt(\n387\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(blob.X-nodePos[0], 2)+\n388\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(blob.Y-nodePos[1], 2)+\n389\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(blob.Z-nodePos[2], 2)) +\n390\t\t\t\tmath.Sqrt(\n391\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[0]-blob.X, 2)+\n392\t\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[1]-blob.Y, int(math.Ceil(deltaL / halfLambda))\n398\t\t\tif zoneNumber < 1 {\n399\t\t\t\tzoneNumber = 1\n400\t\t\t}\n401\t\n402\t\t\t// Zone decay: 1/n^decay_rate, decay_rate=2.0 per plan\n403\t\t\tzoneDecay := zone_decay\n407\t\t\trawContribution := link.DeltaRMS * link.Weight * zoneDecay\n408\t\n409\t\t\tlinkContrib := LinkContribution{\n410\t\t\t\tLinkID:       linkID,\n411\t\t\t\tNodeMAC: contributing,\n417\t\t\t\tContribution: rawContribution, // normalized below\n418\t\t\t}\n419\t\t\texplanation.AllLinks = append(explanation.AllLinks, linkContrib)\n420\t\n421\t\t\tif contributing {\n422\t\t\t\ttotalContribution += rawContribution\n423\t\n424\t\t\t\t// Fresnel zone ellipsoid for contributing link\n425\t\t\t\tcenterX := (nodePos[0] + peerPos[0]) / 2\n426\t\t\t\tcenterY := (nodePos[1] + peerPos[1]) / 2\n427\t\t\t\tcenterZ := (nodePos[2] + peerPos[2]) / 2\n428\t\t\t\t// Semi-major axis along link axis; semi-minor perpendicular\n429\t\t\t\ta := (pathDirect + lambda) / 2\n430\t\t\t\tb := math.Sqrt(math.Max(0, a*a-(pathDirect/2)*(pathDirect/2)))\n431\t\t\t\texplanation.FresnelZones = append(explanation.FresnelZones, FresnelZone{\n432\t\t\t\t\tLinkID:    linkID,\n433\t\t\t\t\tCenterPos: [3]float64{centerX, centerY, centerZ},\n434\t\t\t\t\tSemiAxes:  [3]float64{b, b, a},\n435\t\t\t\t\tZoneNumber: zoneNumber,\n436\t\t\t\t\tTXPos:     nodePos,\n437\t\t\t\t\tRXPos:     peerPos,\n438\t\t\t\t\tLambda:    lambda,\n439\t\t\t\t})\n440\t\t\t}\n441\t\t}\n442\t\n443\t\t// Normalize contributions so contributing links sum to 1.0 (proper percentage breakdown).\n444\t\t// Non-contributing links retain their raw value for display context.\n445\t\tif totalContribution > 0 {\n446\t\t\tfor i := range explanation.AllLinks {\n447\t\t\t\tif normalized AllLinks slice\n454\t\tfor _, lc := range explanation.AllLinks {\n455\t\t\tif lc.Contributing {\n456\t\t\t\texplanation.ContributingLinks = append(explanation.ContributingLinks, -x\n\t}\n\treturn x\n}\n\n// GetExplanationForBlob retrieves the explainability snapshot for a blob at or near a specific timestamp.\n// This is a public method used by other handlers (like feedback) to access explainability data.\nfunc (h *Handler) GetExplanationForBlob(blobID int, timestamp int64) *BlobExplanation {\n\th.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer h.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\t// First try to get by blob ID directly\n\tif explanation, ok := h.blobHistory[blobID]; ok {\n\t\t// Check if the timestamp is close (within 1 minute)\n\t\tif abs64(explanation.Timestamp-timestamp) < 60000 {\n\t\t\treturn explanation\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// If not found by blob ID or timestamp mismatch, search by timestamp\n\t// Find the closest explanation within 1 minute\n\tvar closest *BlobExplanation\n\tminDiff := int64(60000) // 1 minute\n\n\tfor _, exp := range h.blobHistoryByTime {\n\t\tdiff := abs64(exp.Timestamp - timestamp)\n\t\tif diff < minDiff {\n\t\t\tminDiff = diff\n\t\t\tclosest = exp\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif closest != nil {\n\t\treturn closest\n\t}\n\n\t// Return nil if nothing found\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// refreshData handles POST /api/explain/refresh\n// This is called by the dashboard to refresh the explainability data.\nfunc (h *Handler) refreshData(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\tvar req struct {\n\t\tBlobs       []BlobSnapshot    `json:\"blobs\"`\n\t\tLinks       []LinkState      `json:\"links\"`\n\t\tGridData    *GridSnapshot    `json:\"grid_data,omitempty\"`\n\t\tIdentity    map[int]*BLEMatch + link.PeerMAC\n\t\th.linkStates[linkID] = &link\n\t}\n\n\t// Generate explanations for each blob\n\tfor _, blob := range req.Blobs {\n\t\texplanation := h.computeExplanation(blob, req.Links, computation only needs blob/link positions.\nfunc (h *Handler) computeExplanation(blob BlobSnapshot, links []LinkState, _ *GridSnapshot) *BlobExplanation {\n\texplanation := &BlobExplanation{\n\t\tBlobID:            blob.ID,\n\t\tX:                 blob.X,\n\t\tY:                 blob.Y,\n\t\tZ:                 blob.Z,\n\t\tConfidence:        blob.Confidence,\n\t\tContributingLinks: []LinkContribution{},\n\t\tAllLinks:          make([]LinkContribution, 0, len(links)),\n\t\tFresnelZones:      []FresnelZone{},\n\t}\n\n\t// WiFi wavelength constant (2.4 GHz -> ~0.123 m)\n\tconst lambda = 0.123\n\tconst halfLambda = lambda / 2\n\n\tvar totalContribution float64\n\n\t// Compute raw contribution for each link\n\tfor _, link := range links {\n\t\tlinkID := link.NodeMAC + \":\" + link.PeerMAC\n\n\t\tnodePos := [3]float64{link.NodePos[0], link.NodePos[1], link.NodePos[2]}\n\t\tpeerPos := [3]float64{link.PeerPos[0], link.PeerPos[1], link.PeerPos[2]}\n\n\t\t// Path length excess at blob position: ΔL = |blob-TX| + |blob-RX| - |TX-RX|\n\t\tpathDirect := math.Sqrt(\n\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[0]-nodePos[0], 2) +\n\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[1]-nodePos[1], 2) +\n\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[2]-nodePos[2], 2))\n\t\tpathViaBlob := math.Sqrt(\n\t\t\tmath.Pow(blob.X-nodePos[0], 2)+\n\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(blob.Y-nodePos[1], 2)+\n\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(blob.Z-nodePos[2], 2)) +\n\t\t\tmath.Sqrt(\n\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[0]-blob.X, 2)+\n\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[1]-blob.Y, 2)+\n\t\t\t\t\tmath.Pow(peerPos[2]-blob.Z, 2))\n\t\tdeltaL := pathViaBlob - pathDirect\n\n\t\t// Fresnel zone number: zone = ceil(ΔL / (λ/2)), minimum 1\n\t\tzoneNumber := int(math.Ceil(deltaL / halfLambda))\n\t\tif zoneNumber < 1 {\n\t\t\tzoneNumber = 1\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Zone decay: 1/n^decay_rate, decay_rate=2.0 per plan\n\t\tzoneDecay := 1.0 / math.Pow(float64(zoneNumber), 2.0)\n\n\t\tcontributing := link.Motion && link.DeltaRMS > 0.02\n\t\t// Raw contribution = deltaRMS × learned_weight × zone_decay\n\t\trawContribution := link.DeltaRMS * link.Weight * zoneDecay\n\n\t\tlinkContrib := LinkContribution{\n\t\t\tLinkID:       linkID,\n\t\t\tNodeMAC:      link.NodeMAC,\n\t\t\tPeerMAC:      link.PeerMAC,\n\t\t\tDeltaRMS:     link.DeltaRMS,\n\t\t\tZoneNumber:   zoneNumber,\n\t\t\tWeight:       link.Weight,\n\t\t\tContributing: contributing,\n\t\t\tContribution: rawContribution, // normalized below\n\t\t}\n\t\texplanation.AllLinks = append(explanation.AllLinks, linkContrib)\n\n\t\tif contributing {\n\t\t\ttotalContribution += rawContribution\n\n\t\t\t// Fresnel zone ellipsoid for contributing link\n\t\t\tcenterX := (nodePos[0] + peerPos[0]) / 2\n\t\t\tcenterY := (nodePos[1] + peerPos[1]) / 2\n\t\t\tcenterZ := (nodePos[2] + peerPos[2]) / 2\n\t\t\t// Semi-major axis along link axis; semi-minor perpendicular\n\t\t\ta := (pathDirect + lambda) / 2\n\t\t\tb := math.Sqrt(math.Max(0, a*a-(pathDirect/2)*(pathDirect/2)))\n\t\t\texplanation.FresnelZones = append(explanation.FresnelZones, FresnelZone{\n\t\t\t\tLinkID:    linkID,\n\t\t\t\tCenterPos: [3]float64{centerX, centerY, centerZ},\n\t\t\t\tSemiAxes:  [3]float64{b, b, a},\n\t\t\t\tZoneNumber: zoneNumber,\n\t\t\t\tTXPos:     nodePos,\n\t\t\t\tRXPos:     peerPos,\n\t\t\t\tLambda:    lambda,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Normalize contributions so contributing links sum to 1.0 (proper percentage breakdown).\n\t// Non-contributing links retain their raw value for display context.\n\tif totalContribution > 0 {\n\t\tfor i := range explanation.AllLinks {\n\t\t\tif explanation.AllLinks[i].Contributing {\n\t\t\t\texplanation.AllLinks[i].Contribution /= totalContribution\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Populate ContributingLinks from the normalized AllLinks slice\n\tfor _, lc := range explanation.AllLinks {\n\t\tif lc.Contributing {\n\t\t\texplanation.ContributingLinks = append(explanation.ContributingLinks, lc)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn explanation\n}\n\n// BuildWebSocketSnapshot returns an explanation snapshot for a blob in the\n// format expected by the dashboard WebSocket handler (_transformSnapshot in\n// explainability.js). Returns nil if the blob has no recorded explanation.\nfunc (h *Handler) BuildWebSocketSnapshot(blobID int) map[string]interface{} {\n\th.mu.RLock()\n\texp, ok := function _drawSparkline(canvas, points, threshold) {\n296\t        var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');\n297\t        var w = canvas.width;\n298\t        var h = canvas.height;\n299\t        threshold = maxVal) * (h - 6) - 3;\n332\t            ctx.strokeStyle = '#4FC3F7';\n333\t            ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;\n334\t            ctx.beginPath();\n335\t            ctx.moveTo(0, flatY);\n336\t sparkline\n342\t            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(79, 195, 247, 0.12)';\n343\t            ctx.beginPath();\n344\t            for (var i = 0; i < points.length; i++) {\n345\t                var x = i * xStep;\n346\t                var y = h - (points[i] / maxVal) * (h - 6) - 3;\n347\t                if (i === 0) ctx.moveTo(x, h);\n348\t                ctx.lineTo(x, y);\n349\t            }\n350\t _sceneOverlay = null;\n    let _viz3dCallbacks = [];  // Store Viz3D cleanup callbacks\n    let _escKeyHandler = null;\n\n    // ── Configuration contributing links\n        highlightEmissive: 0x555500,\n        fresnelOpacity: 0.25,         // Opacity for Fresnel zones\n        fresnelColor: 0x4FC3F7,       // Blue for Fresnel zones\n        animationDuration: 300,       // ms for scene transitions\n    };\n\n    // ── UI Components ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n    function createSidebarPanel() {\n        var panel = document.createElement('div');\n        panel.id = 'explainability-sidebar';\n        panel.className = 'panel-sidebar panel-sidebar-right';\n        panel.style.display = 'none';\n        panel.innerHTML =\n            '<div class=\"panel-header\">' +\n            '  <h2 class=\"panel-title\">Why is this here?</h2>' +\n            '  <button class=\"panel-close\" onclick=\"Explainability.close()\">&times;</button>' +\n            '</div>' +\n            '<div class=\"panel-content\" id=\"explainability-content\">' +\n            '  <div class=\"explainability-loading\">' +\n            '    <div class=\"panel-loading-spinner\"></div>' +\n            '    <span>Loading explanation...</span>' +\n            '  </div>' +\n            '</div>';\n\n        document.body.appendChild(panel);\n\n        // Create overlay backdrop\n        var backdrop = document.createElement('div');\n        backdrop.id = 'explainability-backdrop';\n        backdrop.className = 'panel-overlay';\n        backdrop.style.display = 'none';\n        backdrop.addEventListener('click', function() {\n            Explainability.close();\n        });\n        document.body.appendChild(backdrop);\n\n        _sidebarPanel = panel;\n        _sceneOverlay = backdrop;\n\n        return panel;\n    }\n\n    function renderContent(data) {\n        var content = document.getElementById('explainability-content');\n        if (!content) return;\n\n        if (!data) {\n            content.innerHTML =\n                '<div class=\"panel-empty\">' +\n                '  <div class=\"panel-empty-icon\">&#128193;</div>' +\n                '  <div class=\"panel-empty-text\">No explanation data available</div>' +\n                '</div>';\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Calculate confidence percentage\n        var confidencePercent = Math.round(data.confidence * 100);\n\n        var html = '';\n\n        // Blob position display\n        if (data.blob_position) {\n            html += '<div class=\"blob-position-display\">' +\n                'Detected at (<span class=\"coord\">' + data.blob_position[0].toFixed(1) + 'm</span>, ' +\n                '<span class=\"coord\">' + data.blob_position[1].toFixed(1) + 'm</span>, ' +\n                '<span class=\"coord\">' + data.blob_position[2].toFixed(1) + 'm</span>)' +\n                '</div>';\n        }\n\n        html += '<div class=\"explainability-confidence\">' +\n            '  <div class=\"confidence-gauge\">' +\n            '    <svg viewBox=\"0 0 36 36\" class=\"confidence-ring\">' +\n            '      <circle class=\"confidence-ring-bg\" cx=\"18\" cy=\"18\" r=\"15\"/>' +\n            '      <circle class=\"confidence-ring-fill\" cx=\"18\" cy=\"18\" r=\"15\" ' +\n            '              style=\"stroke-dasharray: ' + confidencePercent + ' 100\"/>' +\n            '    </svg>' +\n            '    <div class=\"confidence-value\">' + confidencePercent + '%</div>' +\n            '  </div>' +\n            '  <span class=\"confidence-label\">Detection confidence</span>' +\n            '</div>';\n\n        // Contributing links table\n        if (data.contributing_links && data.contributing_links.length > 0) {\n            html += '<div class=\"explainability-section\">' +\n                '  <h3 class=\"section-title\">Contributing Links</h3>' +\n                '  <table class=\"links-table\">' +\n                '    <thead>' +\n                '      <tr>' +\n                '        <th>Link</th>' +\n                '        <th>Contribution</th>' +\n                '        <th>deltaRMS</th>' +\n                '        <th>Zone</th>' +\n                '      </tr>' +\n                '    </thead>' +\n                '    <tbody>';\n\n            data.contributing_links.forEach(function (link) {\n                var zoneColor = _getZoneColor(link.zone_number);\n                var contribPct = Math.round((link.contribution || 0) * 100);\n                html +=\n                    '<tr>' +\n                    '  <td class=\"link-cell\"><code class=\"link-id\">' + _shortenMAC(link.node_mac) + ':' + _shortenMAC(link.peer_mac) + '</code></td>' +\n                    '  <td class=\"contribution-cell\">' + contribPct + '%</td>' +\n                    '  <td class=\"deltarms-cell\">' + link.delta_rms.toFixed(3) + '</td>' +\n                    '  <td class=\"zone-cell\"><span class=\"zone-badge\" style=\"background:' + zoneColor + '\">' + link.zone_number + '</span></td>' +\n                    '</tr>';\n            });\n\n            html += '    </tbody>' +\n                '  </table>' +\n                '</div>';\n\n            // Motion sparklines: 30-second deltaRMS history per contributing link\n            html += '<div class=\"explainability-section\">' +\n                '  <h3 class=\"section-title\">Signal History (30s)</h3>' +\n                '  <div class=\"sparklines-container\" id=\"sparklines-container\">';\n            data.contributing_links.forEach(function (link) {\n                var safeID = 'sparkline-' + link.link_id.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '_');\n                html +=\n                    '<div class=\"sparkline-row\">' +\n                    '  <span class=\"sparkline-label\">' + _shortenMAC(link.node_mac) + ':' + _shortenMAC(link.peer_mac) + '</span>' +\n                    '  <canvas class=\"sparkline-canvas\" id=\"' + safeID + '\"' +\n                    '    width=\"200\" height=\"40\"' +\n                    '    data-link-id=\"' + link.link_id + '\"' +\n                    '    data-delta-rms=\"' + link.delta_rms + '\">' +\n                    '  </canvas>' +\n                    '</div>';\n            });\n            html += '  </div>' +\n                '</div>';\n        }\n\n        // All links (including non-contributing)\n        if (data.all_links && data.all_links.length > 0) {\n            html += '<div class=\"explainability-section collapsed\" id=\"all-links-section\">' +\n                '  <div class=\"section-header toggle-header\" onclick=\"Explainability.toggleSection(this)\">' +\n                '    All Links (' + data.all_links.length + ')' +\n                '    <span class=\"toggle-icon\">▼</span>' +\n                '  </div>' +\n                '  <div class=\"section-content\" style=\"display:none;\">' +\n                '    <table class=\"links-table links-table-detailed\">' +\n                '      <thead>' +\n                '        <tr>' +\n                '          <th>Link</th>' +\n                '          <th>deltaRMS</th>' +\n                '          <th>Zone</th>' +\n                '          <th>Weight</th>' +\n                '          <th>Contribution</th>' +\n                '          <th>Contributing?</th>' +\n                '        </tr>' +\n                '      </thead>' +\n                '      <tbody>';\n\n            data.all_links.forEach(function (link) {\n                var isContributing = link.contributing;\n                var contribClass = isContributing ? 'contributing-yes' : 'contributing-no';\n                var contribText = isContributing ? '✓' : '—';\n\n                html +=\n                    '<tr class=\"' + contribClass + '\">' +\n                    '  <td class=\"link-cell\"><code class=\"link-id\">' + _shortenMAC(link.node_mac) + ':' + _shortenMAC(link.peer_mac) + '</code></td>' +\n                    '  <td class=\"deltarms-cell\">' + link.delta_rms.toFixed(3) + '</td>' +\n                    '  <td class=\"zone-cell\">' + link.zone_number + '</td>' +\n                    '  <td class=\"weight-cell\">' + link.weight.toFixed(2) + '</td>' +\n                    '  <td class=\"contribution-cell\">' + link.contribution.toFixed(4) + '</td>' +\n                    '  <td class=\"contributing-cell\"><span class=\"contributing-badge ' + contribClass + '\">' + contribText + '</span></td>' +\n                    '</tr>';\n            });\n\n            html += '      </tbody>' +\n                '    </table>' +\n                '  </div>' +\n                '</div>';\n        }\n\n        // BLE match section\n        if (data.ble_match) {\n            var ble = data.ble_match;\n            var bleName = ble.person_label || ble.person_id || 'Unknown';\n            var bleConfidence = ble.confidence || ble.triangulation_confidence || 0;\n            var bleDevice = ble.device_addr || ble.device_mac || '';\n            var bleColor = ble.person_color || '#4488ff';\n            html += '<div class=\"explainability-section\">' +\n                '  <h3 class=\"section-title\">BLE Identity Match</h3>' +\n                '  <div class=\"ble-match-card\">' +\n                '    <div class=\"ble-match-header\">' +\n                '      <span class=\"ble-match-indicator\" style=\"background:' + bleColor + '\"></span>' +\n                '      <span class=\"ble-match-name\">' + bleName + '</span>' +\n                '      <span class=\"ble-match-confidence\">' + Math.round(bleConfidence * 100) + '% confident</span>' +\n                '    </div>' +\n                '    <div class=\"ble-match-details\">' +\n                '      <div class=\"ble-match-detail\">' +\n                '        <span class=\"detail-label\">Device:</span>' +\n                '        <code class=\"detail-value\">' + bleDevice + '</code>' +\n                '      </div>';\n\n            if (ble.ble_distance_m !== undefined) {\n                html += '<div class=\"ble-match-detail\">' +\n                    '  <span class=\"detail-label\">Distance:</span>' +\n                    '  <span class=\"detail-value\">' + ble.ble_distance_m.toFixed(1) + 'm from blob</span>' +\n                    '</div>';\n            }\n\n            if (ble.reported_by_nodes && ble.reported_by_nodes.length > 0) {\n                html += '<div class=\"ble-match-detail\">' +\n                    '  <span class=\"detail-label\">Seen by:</span>' +\n                    '  <span class=\"detail-value\">' + ble.reported_by_nodes.join(', ') + '</span>' +\n                    '</div>';\n            }\n\n            html += '    </div>' +\n                '  </div>' +\n                '</div>';\n        } else if (data.all_links && data.all_links.length > 0) {\n            // No BLE match: show \"Unknown\" identity\n            html += '<div class=\"explainability-section\">' +\n                '  <h3 class=\"section-title\">Identity</h3>' +\n                '  <div class=\"ble-match-card\">' +\n                '    <div class=\"ble-match-header\">' +\n                '      <span class=\"ble-match-indicator\" style=\"background:#888\"></span>' +\n                '      <span class=\"ble-match-name\">Unknown</span>' +\n                '      <span class=\"ble-match-confidence\">no BLE device match</span>' +\n                '    </div>' +\n                '  </div>' +\n                '</div>';\n        }\n\n        // Close button at bottom\n        html += '<div class=\"explainability-footer\">' +\n            '  <button class=\"panel-btn panel-btn-primary\" onclick=\"Explainability.close()\">Close</button>' +\n            '</div>';\n\n        content.innerHTML = html;\n    }\n\n    function _shortenMAC(mac) {\n        // Shorten MAC to last 6 characters\n        if (!mac) return '----';\n        if (mac.length <= 8) return mac;\n        return '...' + mac.slice(-8);\n    }\n\n    function _getZoneColor(zoneNumber) {\n        // Color gradient for Fresnel zones\n        var colors = [\n            '#22c55e', // zone 1 - green\n            '#84cc16', // zone 2 - lime\n            '#cddc39', // zone 3 - yellow\n            '#ffeb3b', // zone 4 - orange\n            '#ff9800', // zone 5 - deep orange\n        ];\n        return colors[Math.min(zoneNumber - 1, colors.length - 1)] || '#999';\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Draw a deltaRMS sparkline on a canvas element.\n     * The right edge represents the detection moment.\n     * A horizontal dashed line shows the motion threshold.\n     *\n     * @param {HTMLCanvasElement} canvas\n     * @param {number[]} points - deltaRMS values over 30 s (oldest first)\n     * @param {number} threshold - motion detection threshold (default 0.02)\n     */\n    function _drawSparkline(canvas, points, threshold) {\n        var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');\n        var w = canvas.width;\n        var h = canvas.height;\n        threshold = threshold || 0.02;\n\n        ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);\n\n        // Background\n        ctx.fillStyle = '#1a1a2e';\n        ctx.fillRect(0, 0, w, h);\n\n        var maxVal = threshold * 2;\n        if (points && points.length > 0) {\n            for (var i = 0; i < points.length; i++) {\n                if (points[i] > maxVal) maxVal = points[i];\n            }\n        }\n        maxVal = maxVal || 0.1;\n\n        // Threshold dashed line\n        var threshY = h - (threshold / maxVal) * (h - 6) - 3;\n        ctx.save();\n        ctx.setLineDash([3, 3]);\n        ctx.strokeStyle = '#ff6b6b';\n        ctx.lineWidth = 1;\n        ctx.globalAlpha = 0.7;\n        ctx.beginPath();\n        ctx.moveTo(0, threshY);\n        ctx.lineTo(w, threshY);\n        ctx.stroke();\n        ctx.restore();\n\n        if (!points || points.length < 2) {\n            // Single value: draw a flat line at current level\n            var curVal = (points && points.length === 1) ? points[0] : 0;\n            var flatY = h - (curVal / maxVal) * (h - 6) - 3;\n            ctx.strokeStyle = '#4FC3F7';\n            ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            ctx.moveTo(0, flatY);\n            ctx.lineTo(w - 2, flatY);\n            ctx.stroke();\n        } else {\n            var xStep = (w - 2) / (points.length - 1);\n\n            // Fill area under sparkline\n            ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(79, 195, 247, 0.12)';\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            for (var i = 0; i < points.length; i++) {\n                var x = i * xStep;\n                var y = h - (points[i] / maxVal) * (h - 6) - 3;\n                if (i === 0) ctx.moveTo(x, h);\n                ctx.lineTo(x, y);\n            }\n            ctx.lineTo((points.length - 1) * xStep, h);\n            ctx.closePath();\n            ctx.fill();\n\n            // Sparkline\n            ctx.strokeStyle = '#4FC3F7';\n            ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;\n            ctx.beginPath();\n            for (var i = 0; i < points.length; i++) {\n                var x = i * xStep;\n                var y = h - (points[i] / maxVal) * (h - 6) - 3;\n                if (i === 0) ctx.moveTo(x, y);\n                else ctx.lineTo(x, y);\n            }\n            ctx.stroke();\n        }\n\n        // Detection marker at right edge\n        ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.6)';\n        ctx.lineWidth = 1;\n        ctx.beginPath();\n        ctx.moveTo(w - 1, 0);\n        ctx.lineTo(w - 1, h);\n        ctx.stroke();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Fetch 30-second deltaRMS history for each contributing link and draw sparklines.\n     * Falls back gracefully if the recordings API is unavailable.\n     *\n     * @param {Array} contributingLinks - Array of link contribution objects\n     */\n    function _fetchAndDrawSparklines(contributingLinks) {\n        if (!contributingLinks || contributingLinks.length === 0) return;\n\n        contributingLinks.forEach(function (link) {\n            var safeID = 'sparkline-' + link.link_id.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '_');\n            var canvas = document.getElementById(safeID);\n            if (!canvas) return;\n\n            var deltaRMS = link.delta_rms || 0;\n\n            // Try to fetch 30s history from the recordings API\n            fetch('/api/recordings/' + encodeURIComponent(link.link_id) + '/recent?seconds=30')\n                .then(function (resp) {\n                    if (!resp.ok) throw new Error('no data');\n                    return resp.json();\n                })\n                .then(function (data) {\n                    var points = Array.isArray(data.delta_rms) ? data.delta_rms : [deltaRMS];\n                    _drawSparkline(canvas, points, 0.02);\n                })\n                .catch(function () {\n                    // Fallback: render a flat line at the current deltaRMS value\n                    _drawSparkline(canvas, [deltaRMS], 0.02);\n                });\n        });\n    }\n\n    function toggleSection(header) {\n        var content = header.nextElementSibling;\n        var icon = header.querySelector('.toggle-icon');\n        var parentSection = header.parentElement;\n\n        if (content.style.display === 'none') {\n            content.style.display = 'block';\n            if (icon) icon.textContent = '▲';\n            parentSection.classList.remove('collapsed');\n        } else {\n            content.style.display = 'none';\n            if (icon) icon.textContent = '▼';\n            parentSection.classList.add('collapsed');\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ── 3D Scene Manipulation ─────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n    /**\n     * Apply the X-ray overlay effect to the 3D scene.\n     * Dims non-contributing elements and highlights contributing links.\n     */\n    function applyXRayOverlay(explanationData) {\n        if (!window.Viz3D) return;\n\n        // Save original material states and apply dimming\n        _saveAndDimScene();\n\n        // Highlight contributing links\n        _highlightContributingLinks(explanationData);\n\n        // Render Fresnel zone ellipsoids\n        _renderFresnelZones(explanationData);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Save original material states and dim the scene.\n     */\n    function _saveAndDimScene() {\n        _originalMaterialStates.clear();\n\n        // Dim room elements using Viz3D callback\n        if (window.Viz3D.forEachRoomObject) {\n            Viz3D.forEachRoomObject(function(obj) {\n                _dimObject(obj);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Dim all links first (will highlight contributing ones later)\n        if (window.Viz3D.forEachLink) {\n            Viz3D.forEachLink(function(line, linkID) {\n                _dimObject(line);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Dim non-target blobs\n        if (window.Viz3D.forEachBlob) {\n            Viz3D.forEachBlob(function(obj, blobID) {\n                if (blobID !== _currentBlobID && obj.group) {\n                    _dimObject(obj.group);\n                }\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    function _dimObject(obj) {\n        if (!obj || !obj.material) return;\n\n        var uuid = obj.uuid;\n        if (!uuid) return;\n\n        // Save original state\n        if (!_originalMaterialStates.has(uuid)) {\n            _originalMaterialStates.set(uuid, {\n                opacity: obj.material.opacity,\n                transparent: obj.material.transparent,\n                emissiveIntensity: obj.material.emissiveIntensity || 0\n            });\n            if (obj.material.emissive) {\n                _originalMaterialStates.get(uuid).emissiveColor = obj.material.emissive.getHex();\n            }\n            if (obj.material.color) {\n                _originalMaterialStates.get(uuid).color = obj.material.color.getHex();\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Apply dimming\n        obj.material.opacity = CONFIG.dimOpacity;\n        obj.material.transparent = true;\n        if (obj.material.emissive) {\n            obj.material.emissive.setHex(0x000000);\n            obj.material.emissiveIntensity = 0;\n        }\n        obj.material.needsUpdate = true;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Highlight contributing links with a glowing effect.\n     */\n    function _highlightContributingLinks(explanationData) {\n        if (!explanationData.contributing_links || !window.Viz3D) return;\n\n        explanationData.contributing_links.forEach(function (link) {\n            if (window.Viz3D.highlightLink) {\n                Viz3D.highlightLink(link.link_id, CONFIG.highlightColor, CONFIG.highlightEmissive, 0.8);\n                _highlightedLinks.push(link.link_id);\n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Map a contribution percentage (0-100) to a Fresnel zone color.\n     * Low contribution = pale blue, high contribution = bright yellow.\n     */\n    function _contributionColor(contributionPct) {\n        // Normalize to 0..1 range\n        var t = Math.min(1, Math.max(0, (contributionPct || 0) / 50));\n        // Interpolate from pale blue (0x4FC3F7) to bright yellow (0xFFD700)\n        var r = Math.round(0x4F + t * (0xFF - 0x4F));\n        var g = Math.round(0xC3 + t * (0xD7 - 0xC3));\n        var b = Math.round(0xF7 + t * (0x00 - 0xF7));\n        return (r << 16) | (g << 8) | b;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Render Fresnel zone ellipsoids for contributing links.\n     * Uses the Fresnel module for proper orientation along the link axis.\n     */\n    function _renderFresnelZones(explanationData) {\n        if (!explanationData.fresnel_zones) return;\n\n        // Build a lookup of contribution percentages by link_id for color mapping\n        var contribMap = {};\n        if (explanationData.contributing_links) {\n            explanationData.contributing_links.forEach(function (link) {\n                contribMap[link.link_id] = (link.contribution || 0) * 100;\n            });\n        }\n\n        explanationData.fresnel_zones.forEach(function (zone) {\n            var pct = contribMap[zone.link_id] || 0;\n            var color = _contributionColor(pct);\n\n            // Try the Fresnel module first (proper orientation along link axis)\n            if (window.Fresnel && zone.tx_pos && zone.rx_pos) {\n                var tx = new THREE.Vector3(zone.tx_pos[0], zone.tx_pos[1], zone.tx_pos[2]);\n                var rx = new THREE.Vector3(zone.rx_pos[0], zone.rx_pos[1], zone.rx_pos[2]);\n                // Derive channel from wavelength: 2.4 GHz channels ≤ 14, 5 GHz > 14\n                var channel = zone.lambda <= 0.07 ? 36 : 6;\n                var ellipsoid = Fresnel.addFresnelEllipsoid(tx, rx, channel, color, {\n                    fillOpacity: 0.1,\n                    wireframeOpacity: 0.4\n                });\n                if (ellipsoid) {\n                    _fresnelMeshes.push(ellipsoid);\n                }\n                return;\n            }\n\n            // Fallback to Viz3D (no orientation, but at least shows ellipsoid at center)\n            if (window.Viz3D && Viz3D.addFresnelZone) {\n                var mesh = Viz3D.addFresnelZone(\n                    zone.center_pos[0], zone.center_pos[1], zone.center_pos[2],\n                    zone.semi_axes[0], zone.semi_axes[1], zone.semi_axes[2],\n                    color,\n                    CONFIG.fresnelOpacity\n                );\n                if (mesh) {\n                    _fresnelMeshes.push(mesh);\n                }\n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Restore the scene to its original state.\n     */\n    function restoreScene() {\n        // Restore material states\n        if (window.Viz3D) {\n            _originalMaterialStates.forEach(function (state, uuid) {\n                if (window.Viz3D.restoreObjectMaterial) {\n                    Viz3D.restoreObjectMaterial(uuid, state);\n                }\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Remove Fresnel zone ellipsoids\n        _fresnelMeshes.forEach(function (item) {\n            // Fresnel module returns { wireframe, fill, data } objects\n            if (item && item.wireframe && window.Fresnel) {\n                Fresnel.removeFresnelEllipsoid(item);\n            } else if (item && window.Viz3D) {\n                Viz3D.removeFresnelZone(item);\n            }\n        });\n        _fresnelMeshes = [];\n        _highlightedLinks = [];\n        _originalMaterialStates.clear();\n    }\n\n    // ── API Integration ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n    function fetchExplanation(blobID) {\n        // Send a WebSocket request_explain message. The server will respond\n        // with a blob_explain message on the next fusion tick, which app.js\n        // routes to handleExplainSnapshot().\n        if (window.SpaxelWebSocket && SpaxelWebSocket.send) {\n            SpaxelWebSocket.send(JSON.stringify({\n                type: 'request_explain',\n                blob_id: blobID\n            }));\n        } else {\n            // Fallback to REST API if WebSocket not available\n            fetch('/api/explain/' + encodeURIComponent(blobID))\n                .then(function (response) {\n                    if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to fetch explanation');\n                    return response.json();\n                })\n                .then(function (data) {\n                    _explanationData = data;\n                    renderContent(data);\n                    applyXRayOverlay(data);\n                })\n                .catch(function (error) {\n                    console.error('[Explainability] Failed to load explanation:', error);\n                    renderContent(null);\n                });\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Handle a blob_explain WebSocket message from the fusion engine.\n     * Called by app.js when a {\"type\":\"blob_explain\",...} message arrives.\n     *\n     * @param {number} blobID - The blob ID this snapshot explains\n     * @param {Object} snapshot - The ExplainabilitySnapshot from the server\n     */\n    function handleExplainSnapshot(blobID, snapshot) {\n        // Only process if we're waiting for this blob\n        if (!_isActive || _currentBlobID !== blobID) return;\n\n        _explanationData = _transformSnapshot(snapshot);\n        renderContent(_explanationData);\n        applyXRayOverlay(_explanationData);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Transform the WebSocket ExplainabilitySnapshot into the format\n     * expected by renderContent() and the X-ray overlay.\n     */\n    function _transformSnapshot(snap) {\n        if (!snap) return null;\n\n        var data = {\n            confidence: snap.fusion_score || 0,\n            blob_position: snap.blob_position,\n            contributing_links: [],\n            all_links: [],\n            fresnel_zones: [],\n            ble_match: snap.ble_match || null\n        };\n\n        if (snap.per_link_contributions) {\n            snap.per_link_contributions.forEach(function (link) {\n                var entry = {\n                    link_id: link.link_id,\n                    node_mac: link.tx_mac,\n                    peer_mac: link.rx_mac,\n                    delta_rms: link.delta_rms,\n                    zone_number: link.zone_number,\n                    weight: link.combined_weight,\n                    contribution: link.contribution_pct / 100,\n                    contributing: link.contributing\n                };\n\n                if (link.contributing) {\n
